Build of lapack with android toolchain

The build took 00h 03m 32s and was NOT successful.

The process tree of the build process is here.

Several sub-process invocations were improper; see the process tree for details. Summary:

  • hardcoded invocation:
    • ×4: /usr/sbin/ar
    • ×4: /usr/sbin/ranlib

Due to the failure of this package to build, we did not attempt to build several packages that depend on this one. Those packages are:

  • linbox
  • fflas-ffpack
  • python-cvxopt
  • suitesparse
